If the server returns a 429 (Too Many Requests), the script will automatically pause, wait a little bit, and try again before giving up.\n*   This backoff logic was added to both the **Harvesting module** and the **Global HTTP request helper**, meaning it protects the Scanners and Exploits as well!\n\n### 3.
